    var addClicktracking = function(){
       //Rec A Click tracking
        function tSearchClick(){
            var findHotelsLink = document.querySelector('.searchform .search__container .m-button-l');
            if(findHotelsLink){
                console.log('Rec A here');
                findHotelsLink.addEventListener('click',function() {
                    console.log('clickedLink');
                    mboxName ='tabbedSearchClickedCta_FindHotels';
                    adobe.target.trackEvent(
                        {
                        'mbox':mboxName, 
                        'params': {
                            "ClickedCta": 'FindHotels'
                            }
                        }
                    );
                })
            } 
        }     
        function fragmentLoaded(){
            var navbar = document.querySelector('.m-header__nav');
            if (navbar){
                console.log('Nav loaded');
                clearInterval(checkFragment);
                tSearchClick();
            }else{
                console.log('waiting for the fragment');
            }
        }

        checkFragment = window.setInterval(fragmentLoaded,1000);
    }

    var cancel_interval_tabbed = setInterval(tabbedSearch, 30);
      function tabbedSearch() {
        if (document.readyState == "interactive" && typeof window.s === "object") {
          console.log('DOM is interactive');
          console.log('tabbed Search');
          clearInterval(cancel_interval_tabbed);
          addClicktracking();
        }
        else if (document.readyState == "complete" && typeof window.s === "object") {
          console.log('DOM loaded');
          console.log('tabbed Search');
          clearInterval(cancel_interval_tabbed);
          addClicktracking();
        }
    }

  (function () {
    function getCookie(cname) {
      var name = cname + "=";
      var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
      for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
          c = c.substring(1);
        }
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
          return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
        }
      }
      return "";
    }

    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes) {
      var d = new Date();
      d.setTime(d.getTime() + minutes * 60 * 1000);
      var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
      document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
    }

    function atAddLogoImg() {

      var atImgContainer = '<div class="row"> <div class="col-12 col-md-4 col-lg-6"> <div class="hb__credit-card " style=" height: unset;"> <picture class="lazy-image"> <source media="(min-width: 768px)" srcset="' + atLogoImage + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=' + atLogoImageDeskWidth2X + ':* 2x, ' + atLogoImage + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=' + atLogoImageDeskWidth + ':*" ></source> <source media="(min-width: 1px)" srcset="' + atLogoImage + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=' + atLogoImageMobileWidth2X + ':* 2x, ' + atLogoImage + '?interpolation=progressive-bilinear&downsize=' + atLogoImageMobileWidth + ':*" ></source> <img class="" alt="' + atLogoImageAltCopy + '" src="' + atLogoImage + '"> </picture> </div></div></div>';
      var refNode = document.querySelector('div.searchform + div.experiencefragment.at-element-marker section[id*="herobanner"] > div > div.hb__cnt-sec > div');
      refNode.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", atImgContainer);
    }

    function checkEl() {
      var elExists = document.body.contains(document.querySelector('div.searchform + div.experiencefragment.at-element-marker'));
      if (elExists) {
        document.querySelector('div.searchform + div.experiencefragment.at-element-marker a.m-button-m').setAttribute("custom_click_track_value",atCTAclickTrackVal);
        if (atShowLogo) {
          atAddLogoImg();
        }
      } else {
        window.setTimeout(checkEl, 100);
      }
    }

    function atHeroUpdate() {
      // merchandising impression tracking
      let cname = "merchViewed";
      let cvalue = trackingContentPosition + "-" + trackingDescription;
      let minutes = 30;
      let ctemp = getCookie(cname) || "";
      if (ctemp.includes(cvalue) !== true) {
        if (typeof atCArray !== "object") {
          atCArray = [];
        };
        atCArray.push(cvalue);
      };
      if (typeof atMArray !== "object") {
        atMArray = [];
      }
      atMArray.push('hpHero,type=' + trackingOfferType + ',msg=' + trackingDescription + ',tag=' + trackingTag);
      checkEl();
    }

    // image settings
    let atShowLogo = false; /* false for no logo */
    let atLogoImage = '//www.marriott.com/content/dam/dme/logos/12_16_22_E2L_AEM_SupersizeHero_LogoLight_900x264.png';
    let atLogoImageDeskWidth = 160;
    let atLogoImageDeskWidth2X = atLogoImageDeskWidth * 2;
    let atLogoImageMobileWidth = 120;
    let atLogoImageMobileWidth2X = atLogoImageMobileWidth * 2;
    let atLogoImageAltCopy = 'Marriott Bonvoy Escape to Luxury logo';

    // impression & click tracking values
    let trackingContentPosition = 'hpHero';
    let trackingOfferType =
        'booking'; /* booking, loyalty, cobrand, hvmi, app, toursActivities, multiOffers, content, dine */
    let trackingDescription =
        'demandGen010123'; /* keep short, no spaces (camelCase instead), example escapes1120 */
    let trackingTag =
        'US-demandGen010123'; /* site abbreviation with a dash(-) plus optional values or CX Universal Campaign Code */
    let trackingTag2 =
        'US-cta2'; /* site abbreviation with a dash(-) plus optional values or CX Universal Campaign Code; use to distinguish 2nd CTA clicks */
    let atCTAclickTrackVal = 'HIO|' + trackingDescription + '|external|event167,list3=hpHero;type=' +
        trackingOfferType + ';msg=' + trackingDescription + ';tag=' + trackingTag;

    var atCallback = function () {
      atHeroUpdate();
    };

    if (document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement
                                               .doScroll)) {
      atCallback();
    } else {
      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", atCallback);
    }
  })();

                tryAgain = 50,
                element,
                timer = setInterval(function() {
                    element = document.querySelector(selector)
                    if (element) {
                        callback(element);
                        error = false;
                        tryAgain = 0;
                    }
                    if (--tryAgain < 1) {
                        if (error) {
                            console.log('element was not found');
                        }
                        clearInterval(timer);
                    }
                },200);
        };
  
      function atHpPopularOffersCard1() {
        // updates 4 pack template update

        var x = document.querySelector(".offerscard-dynamic.adobetarget-dynamicoffers-enable section.card-carousel > div.cd-cl > div.glide > div.glide__track.glide__overflow-visible > ul > li:nth-child(1)").getAttribute('style');
        document.querySelector(".offerscard-dynamic.adobetarget-dynamicoffers-enable section.card-carousel > div.cd-cl > div.glide > div.glide__track.glide__overflow-visible > ul > li:nth-child(1)").classList.remove("glide__slide--active");

        let atContentTemplate = '<li class="glide__slide cd-cl__item dynamic-offer-card card-updated glide__slide--active" style="' + x + '"><a id="atHpPopularOffersCard1" class="at-cd-cl__link custom_click_track" custom_click_track_value="' + atCTAclickTrackVal + '" href="' + atCTAurl + '"> <div class="at-cd-cl__image" aria-hidden="true"> <picture class="lazy-image"> <source media="(min-width: 1200px)" srcset=" ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-369x369/image.jpg, ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-738x738/image.jpg 2x"> <source media="(min-width: 992px)" srcset=" ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-309x309/image.jpg, ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-618x618/image.jpg 2x"> <source media="(min-width: 768px)" srcset=" ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-290x290/image.jpg, ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-704x704/image.jpg 2x"> <source media="(max-width: 767.5px)" srcset=" ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-261x261/image.jpg, ' + atImageURL + '.transform/mcom-hp-transform-522x522/image.jpg 2x"> <img class="at-cd-cl__img" alt="' + atImgAltCopy  + '" src="' + atImageURL + '" loading="lazy"/> </picture> </div><div class="at-cd-cl__content" aria-hidden="true"> <div class="at-cd-cl__heading"> <span class="at-cd-cl__card__label t-overline-inverse-normal" >' + atEyeBrowCopy + '</span > <h3 class="at-cd-cl__item-heading t-subtitle-inverse-l">' + atHeaderCopy + '</h3> </div><div class="icon-chevron"><span class="icon-arrow-right"></span></div></div></a></li>';

        var refNode = document.querySelector(".offerscard-dynamic.adobetarget-dynamicoffers-enable section.card-carousel > div.cd-cl > div.glide > div.glide__track.glide__overflow-visible > ul");
        refNode.insertAdjacentHTML("afterbegin", atContentTemplate);
  
        // settings updates
        if (atOpenNewTab == true) {
          document.querySelector('#atHpPopularOffersCard1 a').setAttribute('target', '_blank');
          //document.querySelector('#atHpPopularOffersCard1 a').innerHTML = atCTACopy + '<span aria-label="Opens in a new browser window." class="t-icon-external-site" > </span >';
        }      
      }
  
      var atCallback = function () {
        if (document.querySelector('.herobanner .hb__cta-wrapper a[custom_click_track_value*="' + trackingDescription + '"]') == null) {
        atHpPopularOffersCard1();
        
        // merchandising impression tracking
        let cname = "merchViewed";
        let cvalue = trackingContentPosition + "-" + trackingDescription;

        let ctemp = getCookie(cname) || "";
        if (ctemp.includes(cvalue) !== true) {
          cvalue = ctemp + cvalue + "|";
          setCookie(cname, cvalue, minutes);
        };
        impressionTrack('event168|list3=' + trackingContentPosition + ',type=' + trackingOfferType + ',msg=' + trackingDescription + ',tag=' + trackingTag);
        }
      };
  
      if ( document.readyState === "complete" || (document.readyState !== "loading" && !document.documentElement.doScroll)) {

/*LOAD A SCRIPT WITH A CALLBACK FUNCTION*/
function launchLoadScriptCallback(a, c, b) {
    var d = document.getElementsByTagName("script"),
        e;
    b = d[0];
    for (e = 0; e < d.length; e++)
        if (d[e].src === a && d[e].readyState && /loaded|complete/.test(d[e].readyState)) try {
            c()
        } catch (g) {} finally {
            return
        }
    d = document.createElement("script");
    d.type = "text/javascript";
    d.async = !0;
    d.src = a;
    d.onerror = function() {
        this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded")
    };
    d.onload = d.onreadystatechange = function() {
        if (!this.readyState ||
            "complete" === this.readyState || "loaded" === this.readyState) {
            this.onload = this.onreadystatechange = null;
            this.addEventListener && (this.readyState = "loaded");
            try {
                c.call(this)
            } catch (g) {}
        }
    };
    b.parentNode.insertBefore(d, b)
}

}

    newScript.type = 'text/javascript';
    newScript.src = src; //URL
    newScript.async = (typeof async !== "undefined")?async:true;
    document.head.appendChild(newScript);
}

/*INCLUDE A NEW IFRAME*/
function launchIframe(src) {
    var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
    iframe.style.display = "none";
    iframe.src = src;
    document.body.appendChild(iframe);
}

function getCookie(cname) {
  var name = cname + "=";
  var decodedCookie = decodeURI(document.cookie);
  var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
  for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return "";
}

function sendOptInStatusToAnalytics(){

          obj[split[0].trim()] = split[1].trim();
      }
      console.log(obj.groups.indexOf("6:0"));
      if (obj.groups && obj.groups.indexOf("6:0") != -1) {
          analyticsOptedIn = false;
          console.log("analyticsOptedIn = false");
      } 
      if (obj.groups && obj.groups.indexOf("4:0") != -1) {
          advertOptedIn = false;
          console.log("analyticsOptedIn = false");
      } 
      let advertEvar = advertOptedIn ? "Opted In" : "Opted Out";
      let analyticsEvar = analyticsOptedIn ? "Opted In" : "Opted Out";

      s.linkTrackEvents = "event312";
      s.events = "event312";

      s.tl(this, "o", "Opt_In tracking");
      s.linkTrackEvents = "None";
      s.linkTrackVars = s.origLTV;
      s.events = s.origEvents;
      //_satellite.setVar('overideOptOut', 'false');
  }else{
    console.log("OPT-OUT Failed - sendAnalytics - no OptAnaonCookie");
  } 
}

		return (val === undefined || val == null || val.length <= 0) ? true : false;
	}
	function key(obj) {
		return Object.keys(obj)
		.map(function (k) {
			return k + "" + obj[k];
		})
		.join("");
	}
	function distinct(arr) {
		var result = arr.reduce(function (acc, e) {
			acc[key(e)] = e;
			return acc;
		}, {});
		return Object.keys(result).map(function (k) {
			return result[k];
		});

function mostRecentSearch() {
    var theURL = location.pathname;
    /*** mostRecentSearch() function - extracts values from MDL variable page_url_query_string
     *   on the search results pages. Collects last 5 searches made. Value (Returned as a String) is sent to Adobe Target where  *   it will be then captured in the Profile recent_searches. 
     *   This Profile is used by Web and Mobile.
     ***/
    var srchRad, prpCde;
    var current_recent_searches = localStorage.getItem("recent_searches") || '';
    var noCrrntSrch = true;
    if (current_recent_searches.length > 0) {
        noCrrntSrch = false;
    }
    var current_searches_length = 0;
    if (!noCrrntSrch) {
        current_searches_length = (current_recent_searches.match(/displayName/g) || []).length;
    }
    if ((theURL.indexOf('/search/findHotels') > -1 || theURL.indexOf('/search/default') > -1) && (mdlQS && mdlQS.indexOf("destinationAddress.destination") > -1)) {
        var qsArr = mdlQS.split('&');
        var displayName = qsArr[0].replace("destinationAddress.destination=", '');
        if (current_recent_searches.indexOf(displayName) < 0 || noCrrntSrch) {
            var qsArr = mdlQS.split('&amp;');
            for (var i = 0; i <= qsArr.length; i++) {
                var lastLoop = qsArr.length;
                if (i != lastLoop) {
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("propertyCode=") > -1) {
                        var propertyCode = qsArr[i].replace("propertyCode=", '');
                    }
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.longitude=") > -1) {
                        var longitude = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.longitude=", '');
                    }
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.latitude=") > -1) {
                        var latitude = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.latitude=", '');
                    }
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.stateProvince=") > -1) {
                        var stateProvince = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.stateProvince=", '');
                    }
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("destinationAddress.country=") > -1) {
                        var country = qsArr[i].replace("destinationAddress.country=", '');
                    }
                    if (qsArr[i].indexOf("searchRadius=") > -1) {
                        var searchRadius = qsArr[i].replace("searchRadius=", '');
                    }
                }
            }
            var type = "";
            if (propertyCode != '') {
                type = 'property';
            } else if (propertyCode == '' && stateProvince != '' && country != '') {
                type = 'state';
            } else if (propertyCode == '' && stateProvince == '' && country != '') {
                type = 'country';
            } else {
                type = 'destination';
            }
            //Getting Timestamp
            var dateNow = new Date();
            var timestampNow = dateNow.toISOString();
            var endOfRecord = "";
            if (!noCrrntSrch) {
                endOfRecord = ",";
            }
            var most_recent_search = '{ "displayName":"' + displayName + '" , "propertyCode":"' + propertyCode + '" , "longitude":"' + longitude + '" , "latitude":"' + latitude + '", "stateProvince":"' + stateProvince + '" , "country":"' + country + '" , "searchRadius":"' + searchRadius + '" , "timestamp":"' + timestampNow + '", "type":"' + type + '" }' + endOfRecord;
            if (current_searches_length == 5) {
                var last = current_recent_searches.lastIndexOf(",{");
                var tmpValue = current_recent_searches.slice(last, current_recent_searches.length);
                current_recent_searches = current_recent_searches.replace(tmpValue, '');
            }
            current_recent_searches = most_recent_search + current_recent_searches;
            localStorage.setItem("recent_searches", current_recent_searches);
        }
    }
    return current_recent_searches;
}

function dateDifference(checkInDate) {
    var today = new Date();
    var dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    var mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); //January is 0!
    var yyyy = today.getFullYear();

    today = mm + '/' + dd + '/' + yyyy;
    var startDate = Date.parse(today);
    var endDate = Date.parse(checkInDate);
    var timeDiff = endDate - startDate;
    var daysDiff = Math.floor(timeDiff / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    return daysDiff;
}

var daysToCheckin = 0;

    }
} else {
    if (upcomingCheckInDate != "" && typeof upcomingCheckInDate != "undefined") {
        daysToCheckin = dateDifference(upcomingCheckInDate);
        paramsArray.push("daysToCheckin=" + daysToCheckin);
    }
}

function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1);
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
    return "";
}

        function cookieDel(cname) {
            var d = new Date();
            d.setTime(d.getTime() - (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
            var expires = "expires=" + d.toGMTString();

        function cookieGet(cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }

            return "";
        }

        function bindObjLoad(selector, fn) {
            // Store the selector and callback to be monitored
            listeners.push({
                selector: selector,
                fn: fn
            });
            if (!observer) {
                // Watch for changes in the document
                observer = new MutationObserver(bindObjLoadCheck);
                observer.observe(doc.documentElement, {
                    childList: true,
                    subtree: true
                });
            }
            // bindObjLoadCheck if the element is currently in the DOM
            bindObjLoadCheck();
        }

        function bindOn(selector, type, target, action) {
            switch (type) {
                case 'click':
                case "keyup":
                case "mousedown":
                    bindOnClick(selector, type, target, action);
                    break;
                case 'method':
                    bindOnMethod(selector, type, target, action);
                    break;
            }
        }

        function bindOnClick(selector, type, target, action) {
            var someInput = document.querySelector(selector);
            someInput.addEventListener(type, function(evt) {
                handleClick(evt, target, action);
            });
        }

        function bindOnMethod(obj, actionType, func, args) {
            mart.log('obj : ' + typeof obj);
            mart.log('actionType : ' + actionType);
            mart.log('func : ' + typeof func);
            func.apply(obj, args);
        }

        function handleClick(event, target, action) {
            var someOutput = document.querySelector(target);
            switch (action[0]) {
                case 'style.cssText':
                    someOutput.style.cssText = action[1];
                    break;
                case 'style.setProperty':
                    someOutput.style.setProperty = action[1];
                    break;
                case 'style.background':
                    someOutput.style.background = action[1];
                    break;
                case 'innerHTML':
                    someOutput.innerHTML = action[1];
                    break;
                case 'textContent':
                    someOutput.textContent = action[1];
                    break;
                case 'addClass':
                    someOutput.classList.add(action[1]);
                    break;
                case 'removeClass':
                    someOutput.classList.remove(action[1]);
                    break;
                case 'function':
                    console.log("action1 is " + action[1]);
                    console.log("inside a function @@@@" + typeof action[1]);
                    //console.log(eval(action[1]));
                    eval(action[1]);
                    break;
            }
        }

        function bindObjLoadCheck() {
            // bindObjLoadCheck the DOM for elements matching a stored selector
            for (var i = 0, len = listeners.length, listener, elements; i < len; i++) {
                listener = listeners[i];
                // Query for elements matching the specified selector
                elements = doc.querySelectorAll(listener.selector);
                for (var j = 0, jLen = elements.length, element; j < jLen; j++) {
                    element = elements[j];
                    // Make sure the callback isn't invoked with the
                    // same element more than once
                    if (!element.bindObjLoad) {
                        element.bindObjLoad = true;
                        // Invoke the callback with the element
                        listener.fn.call(element, element);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        /** Custom error log object for Target **/
        if (!window.mart_loglevel) {
            window.mart_loglevel = 0;
        }

                } else {
                    offerLog.push(offrMssg);
                    logList('log', offrListMsg);
                    console.log("MART offerLog in else : " + offerLog);
                }
            }
        }

        function error(mssg) {

        function hashMd5(d) {
            result = M(V(Y(X(d), 8 * d.length)));
            return result.toLowerCase();
        }

        function M(d) {
            for (var _, m = "0123456789ABCDEF", f = "", r = 0; r < d.length; r++) _ = d.charCodeAt(r), f += m.charAt(_ >>> 4 & 15) + m.charAt(15 & _);
            return f;
        }

        function X(d) {
            for (var _ = Array(d.length >> 2), m = 0; m < _.length; m++) _[m] = 0;
            for (m = 0; m < 8 * d.length; m += 8) _[m >> 5] |= (255 & d.charCodeAt(m / 8)) << m % 32;
            return _;
        }

        function V(d) {
            for (var _ = "", m = 0; m < 32 * d.length; m += 8) _ += String.fromCharCode(d[m >> 5] >>> m % 32 & 255);
            return _;
        }

        function md5_cmn(d, _, m, f, r, i) {
            return safe_add(bit_rol(safe_add(safe_add(_, d), safe_add(f, i)), r), m);
        }

        function md5_ff(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {
            return md5_cmn(_ & m | ~_ & f, d, _, r, i, n);
        }

        function md5_gg(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {
            return md5_cmn(_ & f | m & ~f, d, _, r, i, n);
        }

        function md5_hh(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {
            return md5_cmn(_ ^ m ^ f, d, _, r, i, n);
        }

        function md5_ii(d, _, m, f, r, i, n) {
            return md5_cmn(m ^ (_ | ~f), d, _, r, i, n);
        }

        function safe_add(d, _) {
            var m = (65535 & d) + (65535 & _);
            return (d >> 16) + (_ >> 16) + (m >> 16) << 16 | 65535 & m;
        }

        function bit_rol(d, _) {
            return d << _ | d >>> 32 - _;
        }

        function hashSha256(ascii) {
            function rightRotate(value, amount) {
                return (value >>> amount) | (value << (32 - amount));
            }

            var mathPow = Math.pow;
            var maxWord = mathPow(2, 32);
            var lengthProperty = 'length';
            var i, j; // Used as a counter across the whole file
            var result = '';

            var words = [];
            var asciiBitLength = ascii[lengthProperty] * 8;

            //* caching results is optional - remove/add slash from front of this line to toggle
            // Initial hash value: first 32 bits of the fractional parts of the square roots of the first 8 primes
            // (we actually calculate the first 64, but extra values are just ignored)
            var hash = hashSha256.h = hashSha256.h || [];
            // Round constants: first 32 bits of the fractional parts of the cube roots of the first 64 primes
            var k = hashSha256.k = hashSha256.k || [];
            var primeCounter = k[lengthProperty];
            /*/
            var hash = [], k = [];
            var primeCounter = 0;
            //*/

            var isComposite = {};
            for (var candidate = 2; primeCounter < 64; candidate++) {
                if (!isComposite[candidate]) {
                    for (i = 0; i < 313; i += candidate) {
                        isComposite[i] = candidate;
                    }
                    hash[primeCounter] = (mathPow(candidate, 0.5) * maxWord) | 0;
                    k[primeCounter++] = (mathPow(candidate, 1 / 3) * maxWord) | 0;
                }
            }

            ascii += '\x80'; // Append ' bit (plus zero padding)
            while (ascii[lengthProperty] % 64 - 56) ascii += '\x00';
            for (i = 0; i < ascii[lengthProperty]; i++) {
                j = ascii.charCodeAt(i);
                if (j >> 8) return; // ASCII check: only accept characters in range 0-255
                words[i >> 2] |= j << ((3 - i) % 4) * 8;
            }
            words[words[lengthProperty]] = ((asciiBitLength / maxWord) | 0);
            words[words[lengthProperty]] = (asciiBitLength);

            // process each chunk
            for (j = 0; j < words[lengthProperty];) {
                var w = words.slice(j, j += 16); // The message is expanded into 64 words as part of the iteration
                var oldHash = hash;
                // This is now the undefinedworking hash", often labelled as variables a...g
                // (we have to truncate as well, otherwise extra entries at the end accumulate
                hash = hash.slice(0, 8);

                for (i = 0; i < 64; i++) {
                    var i2 = i + j;
                    // Expand the message into 64 words
                    // Used below if 
                    var w15 = w[i - 15],
                        w2 = w[i - 2];

                    // Iterate
                    var a = hash[0],
                        e = hash[4];
                    var temp1 = hash[7] + (rightRotate(e, 6) ^ rightRotate(e, 11) ^ rightRotate(e, 25)) + ((e & hash[5]) ^ ((~e) & hash[6])) + k[i] + (w[i] = (i < 16) ? w[i] : (w[i - 16] + (rightRotate(w15, 7) ^ rightRotate(w15, 18) ^ (w15 >>> 3)) + w[i - 7] + (rightRotate(w2, 17) ^ rightRotate(w2, 19) ^ (w2 >>> 10))) | 0);
                    // This is only used once, so *could* be moved below, but it only saves 4 bytes and makes things unreadble
                    var temp2 = (rightRotate(a, 2) ^ rightRotate(a, 13) ^ rightRotate(a, 22)) + ((a & hash[1]) ^ (a & hash[2]) ^ (hash[1] & hash[2])); // maj

                    hash = [(temp1 + temp2) | 0].concat(hash); // We don't bother trimming off the extra ones, they're harmless as long as we're truncating when we do the slice()
                    hash[4] = (hash[4] + temp1) | 0;
                }

                for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
                    hash[i] = (hash[i] + oldHash[i]) | 0;
                }
            }

            for (i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
                for (j = 3; j + 1; j--) {
                    var b = (hash[i] >> (j * 8)) & 255;
                    result += ((b < 16) ? 0 : '') + b.toString(16);
                }
            }
            return result;
        }

        return {
            trackBehaviorInit: trackBehaviorInit,
            trackMonetate: trackMonetate,
            bindObjLoad: bindObjLoad,
            bindOn: bindOn,
            log: log,
            error: error,
            logList: logList,
            hashMd5: hashMd5,
            hashSha256: hashSha256,
            cookieDel: cookieDel,
            cookieGet: cookieGet,
            cookieSet: cookieSet
        };
    })();

    var tempLists = "";
    var tempLinkTrackVars = "";
    var tempLinkTrackEvents = "";

    s.origLTV = s.linkTrackVars;
    s.origLTE = s.linkTrackEvents;
    s.origEvents = s.events;
    s.linkTrackVars="";
    s.linkTrackEvents="";
    s.events="";

    /*check for events, evars, props*/
    if (typeof x != "undefined") {
        /*check capitalization of event, eVar, prop*/
        var regexE = /event/i;
        var regexV = /evar/i;
        var regexP = /prop/i;
        var regexL = /list/i;
        tempEvents = x.split("^");
        tempEvents.forEach(function(value, index) {
            /*test which variable type*/
            var varType = "";
            if (/^event/i.test(value) == true) {
                varType = "event";
            } else if (/^evar/i.test(value) == true) {
                varType = "eVar";
            } else if (/^prop/i.test(value) == true) {
                varType = "prop";
            } else if (/^list/i.test(value) == true) {
                varType = "list";
            }
            switch (varType) {
                case "event":
                    var eventVal = value.replace(regexE, "event");
                    s.events = s.apl(s.events, eventVal, ",", 2);
                    /*grab only the event name in case there is an incrementor also passed*/
                    var eventName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");
                    tempLinkTrackEvents = s.apl(tempLinkTrackEvents, eventName[0], ",", 2);
                    break;
                case "eVar":
                    /*split the evar and value*/
                    var varName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");
                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, varName[0].replace(regexV, "eVar"), ",", 2);
                    s[varName[0].replace(regexV, "eVar")] = varName[1];
                    break;
                case "prop":
                    /*split the prop and value*/
                    var propName = value.replace("=","@@").split("@@");
                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, propName[0].replace(regexP, "prop"), ",", 2);
                    s[propName[0].replace(regexP, "prop")] = propName[1];
                    break;
                case "list":
                    /*split the prop and value*/
                    var listName = value.replace("=", "@@").split("@@");
                    tempLinkTrackVars = s.apl(tempLinkTrackVars, listName[0].replace(regexL, "list"), ",", 2);
                    s[listName[0].replace(regexL, "list")] = listName[1].replace(/\^/g, "|").replace(/\;/g, ",");
                    break;
                default:
                    // add nothing
            }
        });
    }
    s.linkTrackEvents = tempLinkTrackEvents;
    s.linkTrackVars = tempLinkTrackVars;
    s.tl(this, "o", "Custom Analytics Call");
    s.events = s.origEvents;
    s.linkTrackVars = s.origLTV;
    s.linkTrackEvents = s.origLTE;
}

	let expires = '';

		const date = new Date();

		expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString();

	document.cookie = name + '=' + (value || '') + expires + ';' + 'path=/;';
}

/** Check environment variables first -if they exist setInterval for next round of checks **/
function getParameterByName(name, url = window.location.href) {
    name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, '\\$&');
    var regex = new RegExp('[?&]' + name + '(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)'),
        results = regex.exec(url);
    if (!results) return null;
    if (!results[2]) return '';
    return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
}
/** check for existence of 'AT' query string param and 'CONNECT' value **/
let atQParam = getParameterByName('AT');
let paramPassed = true;
if(atQParam !==null && atQParam =='CONNECT'){
	paramPassed = false;
}

if(
	(_satellite.getVar('env_is_prod')!='undefined' && _satellite.getVar('env_is_prod')=='false') 
	&& (_satellite.getVar('page_pathname')!='undefined' 
        && (_satellite.getVar('page_pathname').includes('einterface')||_satellite.getVar('page_pathname').includes('/hotels/')))
	&& paramPassed
){
	//checkConditions();
}

function checkConditions(){
	if(conditions()){
		/** All conditions passed fire MMN ads **/
		mmnPlacements();
	}else{
		var checker = setInterval(function () {
			if (conditions()) {
				mmnPlacements(); 
				clearInterval(checker);
			} else {
			}
		}, 500);

		var optOutExpiration = setTimeout(function () {
			clearInterval(checker);
		}, 5 * 1000);
	}
}

/** Second set conditionals 
_satellite.getVar('user_optin_status')!='undefined' && _satellite.getVar('user_optin_status')=='optin') && document.getElementsByClassName('mmn-ads-container')[0].getAttribute("data-pos-id-desktop") !== null)         
**/

	let returnVal = false;
 if(document.getElementsByClassName('mmn-ads-container')[0].getAttribute("data-pos-id-desktop") !== null){
		returnVal = true;
	}
  
	return returnVal;
}
